    "file = open('Group1.txt','r',encoding='utf-8')\n",
    "data=file.read()\n",

   "source": [
    "def Remove_StopWords(x):\n",
    "    f=open('App-Files/StopWords.txt','r')\n",
    "    stopWords= f.read().split(\"\\n\")\n",
    "    # links=\" \".join(links)\n",
    "    y = []\n",
    "    if x!=\"This message was deleted\" and x!=\"<Media omitted>\" and x!='You deleted this message':\n",
    "        for word in x.split():\n",
    "            if word.lower() not in stopWords:\n",
    "                y.append(word)\n",
    "    return \" \".join(y)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def split_user(x):\n",
    "    x=x.split(': ',1)\n",
    "    if x[1:]:\n",
    "        return x\n",
    "    \n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        return(['group notification',x[0]])\n",
    "\n",
    "df['User']=df['Messages'].apply(lambda x: split_user(x)[0])\n",
    "df['Messages']= df['Messages'].apply(lambda x: split_user(x)[1])\n",
    "\n",
    "df['text'] = df['Messages'].apply(lambda x : Remove_StopWords(x))\n",
    "df.head()"
   ]
  },

   "source": [
    "import nltk\n",
    "nltk.download('stopwords')\n",
    "#clean the data\n",
    "stop = set(stopwords.words('english'))\n",
    "exclude = set(string.punctuation)\n",
    "lemma = WordNetLemmatizer()\n",
    "\n",
    "def clean(text):\n",
    "    stop_free = ' '.join([word for word in text.lower().split() if word not in stop])\n",
    "    punc_free = ''.join(ch for ch in stop_free if ch not in exclude)\n",
    "    normalized = ' '.join([lemma.lemmatize(word) for word in punc_free.split()])\n",
    "    return normalized.split()\n",
    "df['text_clean']=df['text'].apply(clean)"
   ]
  },
